\ Masterlist Syntax Notes
\
\ Although two syntaxes (MF1 & MF2) are available, only the most common parts of the more general syntax (MF1) is covered here.
\ See the BOSS Masterlist Syntax.html documentation file in data/boss-common/ on the Google Code repository for full details.
\
\  * Use blank lines to separate mods that are grouped together or where it helps readability.
\  * Use silent comments when you think something needs clarification to others reading the masterlist (such as when a mod looks like it is misspelled, but is correct).
\  * Only make edits/additions you're confident about - otherwise discuss the issue on the official forum threads.
\  * If you're unsure on how to write something in the correct syntax, check the masterlists for examples, and don't be afraid to ask other committers for help.
\  * When you include a web link in a message, enclose it in double quotes "", for example: www.example.org should be written "www.example.org".
\  * When you list Bash Tags for a mod, separate them using ", " and not just ",". Eg. {{BASH: Graphics,NoMerge}} should be written {{BASH: Graphics, NoMerge}}. This improves readability in the BOSSlog and the masterlist itself.
\  * Don't include any HTML formatting in messages. In particular, web links do not need to be formatted as HTML hyperlinks, as BOSS will do this automatically.
\  * Don't duplicate lines using different syntaxes. A line only needs to be written in one syntax.
\  * As the majority of BOSS users use versions that only support MF1, write in that where possible.
\
\ Comment Type                      Symbol      Description
\ =====================================================================
\ Silent comment                    \           A silent comment, ignored by BOSS.
\ General comment                   ?           A general comment for the mod above.
\ Bash Tag suggestion               %           A Bash Tag suggestion for the mod above.
\ Requirement                       :           An installation requirement for the mod above.
\ Incompatibility                   "           A specific incompatibility for the mod above.
\ OOO-specific comment              $           A comment that is only displayed if OOO is installed.
\ Better Cities-specific comment    ^           A comment that is only displayed if Better Cities is installed.
\ Critical FCOM install error       >*          Prints an error message if FCOM is installed.
\
\ The symbol is followed by a space then the message string.
\
\ Conditional Type			Symbol		Description
\ ===================================================================================
\ FCOM-installed line			>		Only parses the line if FCOM is installed.
\ FCOM-not-installed line		<		Only parses the line if FCOM is not installed.
\
\ Conditionals can be put before any mod or message line, and the line will only be processed if the conditional is true.
\ The critical FCOM install error message type already includes the FCOM-specific conditional, so you don't need to add another.

\ Masterlist variable setup for BOSS v1.7+.
 IF ("Oscuro's_Oblivion_Overhaul.esm") SET: OOO
 IF ("Better Cities Resources.esm") SET: BC
 IF ("FCOM_Convergence.esm") SET: FCOM
\ The second check is a hack until BOSS 1.9's release.

\ Upgrade message for 1.7+ users:
 IF (<2.0.1.0|"BOSS") GLOBAL WARN: An update for BOSS (v2.0.1) has been released. Download it at "http://oblivion.nexusmods.com/mods/20516", "http://skyrim.nexusmods.com/downloads/file.php?id=6", "http://fallout3.nexusmods.com/mods/10193" or "http://newvegas.nexusmods.com/mods/35999"
 ELSE GLOBAL SAY: You are using the latest version of BOSS.

\BeginGroup\: BSA tricks
\----------

Better Cities .esp
? Dummy file to load Better Cities .BSA
BSAloader.esp
? Dummy file to load .BSA files.
FraNewItems.esp
? Dummy file to load FraNewItems.BSA. Using a file to load a BSA means the BSA must NOT be listed in Oblivion.ini at the same time or the game will not load.
? This is ususally only a problem when automatic installers insert the name into Oblivion.ini then the user creates a BSA redirection file later.
Fra.esp
? Dummy file to load Frans BSA(s). Usually refers to FraNewItems.BSA. Using a file to load a BSA means the BSA must NOT be listed in Oblivion.ini at the same time or the game will not load.
? This is ususally only a problem when automatic installers insert the name into Oblivion.ini then the user creates a BSA redirection file later.
Francesco.esp
? Dummy file to load both Frans BSAs. Using a file to load a BSA means the BSA must NOT be listed in Oblivion.ini at the same time or the game will not load.
? This is ususally only a problem when automatic installers insert the name into Oblivion.ini then the user creates a BSA redirection file later.
Francesco's Creatures and Items Resources.esp
? Dummy file to load both Frans BSAs. Using a file to load a BSA means the BSA must NOT be listed in Oblivion.ini at the same time or the game will not load.
? This is ususally only a problem when automatic installers insert the name into Oblivion.ini then the user creates a BSA redirection file later.
MMM.esp
? Dummy file to load the MMM .BSA.
Oblivion.esp
? Usually a BSA redirection hack. Using a file to load a BSA means the BSA must NOT be listed in Oblivion.ini at the same time or the game will not load.
? This is ususally only a problem when automatic installers insert the name into Oblivion.ini then the user creates a BSA redirection file later.
TamRes.esp
? Dummy file to load the TamRes BSA.
\EndGroup\\
